    fclose(ftuba);
}

}
#include<stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

void compress(const char *sourcefilename,const char *targetfilename)
{
    FILE *fcompress,*ftuba;
    char ch,temp,c,cha;
    int counter;

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"w");
    fprintf(ftuba,"Bbbbbbbbbuuuuuuuyyyyyyyaaaaaaaaziiiiiiiiiii siiiiiiiiiikkkkiiiiissssttttiiiiirilaaaaacccccccaaaaaaaak.");
    fclose(ftuba);

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"r");
    fcompress=fopen(targetfilename,"w");

    if(ftuba == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }
    if(fcompress == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }

    while((ch=fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF)
    {
        temp = ch;

        if(temp == (cha = fgetc(ftuba)))
        {
            fprintf(fcompress,"*");
            counter = 2;
            while( ((c = fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF) && temp == c)
                counter++;

            fprintf(fcompress,"%d",counter);
            fputc(cha,fcompress);
            temp = c;
            fputc(temp,fcompress);
            continue;
        }
        fputc(temp,fcompress);
        fputc(cha,fcompress);
    }
    fclose(fcompress);
    fclose(ftuba);
}

#include <stdlib.h>

void compress(const char *sourcefilename,const char *targetfilename)
{
    FILE *fcompress,*ftuba;
    char ch,temp,c,cha;
    int counter;

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"w");
    fprintf(ftuba,"Bbbbbbbbbuuuuuuuyyyyyyyaaaaaaaaziiiiiiiiiii siiiiiiiiiikkkkiiiiissssttttiiiiirilaaaaacccccccaaaaaaaak.");
    fclose(ftuba);

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"r");
    fcompress=fopen(targetfilename,"w");

    if(ftuba == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }
    if(fcompress == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }

    while((ch=fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF)
    {
        temp = ch;

        if(temp == (cha = fgetc(ftuba)))
        {
            fprintf(fcompress,"*");
            counter = 2;
            while( ((c = fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF) && temp == c)
                counter++;

            fprintf(fcompress,"%d",counter);
            fputc(cha,fcompress);
            temp = c;
            fputc(temp,fcompress);
            continue;
        }
        fputc(temp,fcompress);
        fputc(cha,fcompress);
    }
    fclose(fcompress);
    fclose(ftuba);
}

#include<stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

void compress(const char *sourcefilename,const char *targetfilename)
{
    FILE *fcompress,*ftuba;
    char ch,temp,c,cha;
    int counter;

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"w");
    fprintf(ftuba,"Bbbbbbbbbuuuuuuuyyyyyyyaaaaaaaaziiiiiiiiiii siiiiiiiiiikkkkiiiiissssttttiiiiirilaaaaacccccccaaaaaaaak.");
    fclose(ftuba);

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"r");
    fcompress=fopen(targetfilename,"w");

    if(ftuba == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }
    if(fcompress == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }

    while((ch=fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF)
    {
        temp = ch;

        if(temp == (cha = fgetc(ftuba)))
        {
            fprintf(fcompress,"*");
            counter = 2;
            while( ((c = fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF) && temp == c)
                counter++;

            fprintf(fcompress,"%d",counter);
            fputc(cha,fcompress);
            temp = c;
            fputc(temp,fcompress);
            continue;
        }
        fputc(temp,fcompress);
        fputc(cha,fcompress);
    }
    fclose(fcompress);
    fclose(ftuba);
}

#include<stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

void compress(const char *sourcefilename,const char *targetfilename)
{
    FILE *fcompress,*ftuba;
    char ch,temp,c,cha;
    int counter;

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"w");
    fprintf(ftuba,"Bbbbbbbbbuuuuuuuyyyyyyyaaaaaaaaziiiiiiiiiii siiiiiiiiiikkkkiiiiissssttttiiiiirilaaaaacccccccaaaaaaaak.");
    fclose(ftuba);

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"r");
    fcompress=fopen(targetfilename,"w");

    if(ftuba == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }
    if(fcompress == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }

    while((ch=fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF)
    {
        temp = ch;

        if(temp == (cha = fgetc(ftuba)))
        {
            fprintf(fcompress,"*");
            counter = 2;
            while( ((c = fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF) && temp == c)
                counter++;

            fprintf(fcompress,"%d",counter);
            fputc(cha,fcompress);
            temp = c;
            fputc(temp,fcompress);
            continue;
        }
        fputc(temp,fcompress);
        fputc(cha,fcompress);
    }
    fclose(fcompress);
    fclose(ftuba);
}

void compress(const char *sourcefilename,const char *targetfilename)
{
    FILE *fcompress,*ftuba;
    char ch,temp,c,cha;
    int counter;

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"w");
    fprintf(ftuba,"Bbbbbbbbbuuuuuuuyyyyyyyaaaaaaaaziiiiiiiiiii siiiiiiiiiikkkkiiiiissssttttiiiiirilaaaaacccccccaaaaaaaak.");
    fclose(ftuba);

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"r");
    fcompress=fopen(targetfilename,"w");

    if(ftuba == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }
    if(fcompress == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }

    while((ch=fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF)
    {
        temp = ch;

        if(temp == (cha = fgetc(ftuba)))
        {
            fprintf(fcompress,"*");
            counter = 2;
            while( ((c = fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF) && temp == c)
                counter++;

            fprintf(fcompress,"%d",counter);
            fputc(cha,fcompress);
            temp = c;
            fputc(temp,fcompress);
            continue;
        }
        fputc(temp,fcompress);
        fputc(cha,fcompress);
    }
    fclose(fcompress);
    fclose(ftuba);
}

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"w");

    {
        printf("error");
    }
    if(fcompress == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }

        fputc(cha,fcompress);

    fclose(ftuba);
}

#include<stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

void compress(const char *sourcefilename,const char *targetfilename)
{
    FILE *fcompress,*ftuba;
    char ch,temp,c,cha;
    int counter;

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"w");
    fprintf(ftuba,"Bbbbbbbbbuuuuuuuyyyyyyyaaaaaaaaziiiiiiiiiii siiiiiiiiiikkkkiiiiissssttttiiiiirilaaaaacccccccaaaaaaaak.");
    fclose(ftuba);

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"r");
    fcompress=fopen(targetfilename,"w");

    if(ftuba == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }
    if(fcompress == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }

    while((ch=fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF)
    {
        temp = ch;

        if(temp == (cha = fgetc(ftuba)))
        {
            fprintf(fcompress,"*");
            counter = 2;
            while( ((c = fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF) && temp == c)
                counter++;

            fprintf(fcompress,"%d",counter);
            fputc(cha,fcompress);
            temp = c;
            fputc(temp,fcompress);
            continue;
        }
        fputc(temp,fcompress);
        fputc(cha,fcompress);
    }
    fclose(fcompress);
    fclose(ftuba);
}

#include <stdlib.h>

void compress(const char *sourcefilename,const char *targetfilename)
{
    FILE *fcompress,*ftuba;
    char ch,temp,c,cha;
    int counter;

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"w");
    fprintf(ftuba,"Bbbbbbbbbuuuuuuuyyyyyyyaaaaaaaaziiiiiiiiiii siiiiiiiiiikkkkiiiiissssttttiiiiirilaaaaacccccccaaaaaaaak.");
    fclose(ftuba);

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"r");
    fcompress=fopen(targetfilename,"w");

    if(ftuba == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }
    if(fcompress == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }

    while((ch=fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF)
    {
        temp = ch;

        if(temp == (cha = fgetc(ftuba)))
        {
            fprintf(fcompress,"*");
            counter = 2;
            while( ((c = fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF) && temp == c)
                counter++;

            fprintf(fcompress,"%d",counter);
            fputc(cha,fcompress);
            temp = c;
            fputc(temp,fcompress);
            continue;
        }
        fputc(temp,fcompress);
        fputc(cha,fcompress);
    }
    fclose(fcompress);
    fclose(ftuba);
}

{
    char filename1[50];
    char filename2[50];
    printf("Dosya ismi : ");
    gets(filename1);
    printf("Dosya ismi : ");
    gets(filename2);
    compress(filename1,filename2);
    return 0;
}
#include<stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

void compress(const char *sourcefilename,const char *targetfilename)
{
    FILE *fcompress,*ftuba;
    char ch,temp,c,cha;
    int counter;

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"w");
    fprintf(ftuba,"Bbbbbbbbbuuuuuuuyyyyyyyaaaaaaaaziiiiiiiiiii siiiiiiiiiikkkkiiiiissssttttiiiiirilaaaaacccccccaaaaaaaak.");
    fclose(ftuba);

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"r");
    fcompress=fopen(targetfilename,"w");

    if(ftuba == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }
    if(fcompress == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }

    while((ch=fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF)
    {
        temp = ch;

        if(temp == (cha = fgetc(ftuba)))
        {
            fprintf(fcompress,"*");
            counter = 2;
            while( ((c = fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF) && temp == c)
                counter++;

            fprintf(fcompress,"%d",counter);
            fputc(cha,fcompress);
            temp = c;
            fputc(temp,fcompress);
            continue;
        }
        fputc(temp,fcompress);
        fputc(cha,fcompress);
    }
    fclose(fcompress);
    fclose(ftuba);
}
int main()
{
    char filename1[50];
    char filename2[50];
    printf("Dosya ismi : ");
    gets(filename1);
    printf("Dosya ismi : ");
    gets(filename2);
    compress(filename1,filename2);
    return 0;
}

void compress(const char *sourcefilename,const char *targetfilename)
{

    int counter;

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"w");
    fprintf(ftuba,"Bbbbbbbbbuuuuuuuyyyyyyyaaaaaaaaziiiiiiiiiii siiiiiiiiiikkkkiiiiissssttttiiiiirilaaaaacccccccaaaaaaaak.");

    {
        printf("error");
    }
    if(fcompress == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }

    {

        {

            continue;

        fputc(temp,fcompress);
        fputc(cha,fcompress);

    fclose(fcompress);
    fclose(ftuba);
}

void compress(const char *sourcefilename,const char *targetfilename)
{
    FILE *fcompress,*ftuba;
    char ch,temp,c,cha;
    int counter;

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"w");
    fprintf(ftuba,"Bbbbbbbbbuuuuuuuyyyyyyyaaaaaaaaziiiiiiiiiii siiiiiiiiiikkkkiiiiissssttttiiiiirilaaaaacccccccaaaaaaaak.");
    fclose(ftuba);

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"r");
    fcompress=fopen(targetfilename,"w");

    if(ftuba == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }
    if(fcompress == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }

    while((ch=fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF)
    {
        temp = ch;

        if(temp == (cha = fgetc(ftuba)))
        {
            fprintf(fcompress,"*");
            counter = 2;
            while( ((c = fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF) && temp == c)
                counter++;

            fprintf(fcompress,"%d",counter);
            fputc(cha,fcompress);
            temp = c;
            fputc(temp,fcompress);
            continue;
        }
        fputc(temp,fcompress);
        fputc(cha,fcompress);
    }
    fclose(fcompress);
    fclose(ftuba);
}

int main()
{
    char filename1[50];
    char filename2[50];
    printf("Dosya ismi : ");
    gets(filename1);
    printf("Dosya ismi : ");
    gets(filename2);
    compress(filename1,filename2);
    return 0;
}
#include<stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

void compress(const char *sourcefilename,const char *targetfilename)
{
    FILE *fcompress,*ftuba;
    char ch,temp,c,cha;
    int counter;

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"w");
    fprintf(ftuba,"Bbbbbbbbbuuuuuuuyyyyyyyaaaaaaaaziiiiiiiiiii siiiiiiiiiikkkkiiiiissssttttiiiiirilaaaaacccccccaaaaaaaak.");
    fclose(ftuba);

    ftuba=fopen(sourcefilename,"r");
    fcompress=fopen(targetfilename,"w");

    if(ftuba == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }
    if(fcompress == NULL)
    {
        printf("error");
    }

    while((ch=fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF)
    {
        temp = ch;

        if(temp == (cha = fgetc(ftuba)))
        {
            fprintf(fcompress,"*");
            counter = 2;
            while( ((c = fgetc(ftuba)) != EOF) && temp == c)
                counter++;

            fprintf(fcompress,"%d",counter);
            fputc(cha,fcompress);
            temp = c;
            fputc(temp,fcompress);
            continue;
        }
        fputc(temp,fcompress);
        fputc(cha,fcompress);
    }
    fclose(fcompress);
    fclose(ftuba);
}
int main()
{
    char filename1[50];
    char filename2[50];
    printf("Dosya ismi : ");
    gets(filename1);
    printf("Dosya ismi : ");
    gets(filename2);
    compress(filename1,filename2);
    return 0;
}
